[30;1m388 | [0m[35m<p>You‚Äôll notice the new ‚Äúcmdopts‚Äù decorator. Let‚Äôs say that you have[0m
[30;1m389 | [0m[35msensitive information like a password that you don‚Äôt want to include[0m
[30;1m390 | [0m[35min your pavement. You can easily make it a command line option for that[0m
